# Implementation Progress

Last updated: 2026-07-19 (session 95 — community-visibility ladder: City Heartbeat + both feeds widen window/radius honestly instead of showing empty today+15km slices; migrations `202607190001/02/03` applied to live DB; Cloud Run `defpedal-api-00120-7zw` → `defpedal-api-00121-49h`; E2E verified on production. Earlier: session 94c — error-log #70: nudge location resolver couldn't parse PostgREST's WKB-hex geography serialisation, so EVERY user silently fell to the Bucharest fallback (a rider got a "Bucharest" pulse from a different town; the nudge safety floor gated on Bucharest weather fleet-wide since session 62). WKB decoder added + 12 tests pinning production bytes; deployed `defpedal-api-00118-kzk`. Session 94b — City Riders Pulse recalibrated after Victor's first live notification: RO share cut 60% (Bucharest ~137k → ~55k same conditions) + mediocre-weather factor now grades continuously ×1.0→×0.4 by worst forecast dimension instead of flat ×0.6; deployed Cloud Run `defpedal-api-00117-5zf`. Session 94 (07-18) — cycling-weather notification cadence randomized: 12h–120h random intervals + day-3 inactivity escalation, replacing the fixed daily 8:30 local ping; shipped to Firebase early-access-preview as v0.2.117 build 120, device verification CONFIRMED by Victor 07-19. Earlier: session 93c — Android push delivery restored FLEET-WIDE, error-log #69: Expo had FCM V1 keys for NO Android package, so Android server-push deliveries were ~zero for the app's entire history (notification_log 8,669 failed vs 441 sent; the few successes were iOS/APNs). Preview + production identifiers now configured on expo.dev with the firebase-adminsdk-fbsvc key; verified on device (preview) and via per-token tickets+receipts (production); dev left unconfigured; NEVER EAS-build Android — the wizard-mandated keystore is a throwaway placeholder. ~450 tokens become deliverable from the next cron ticks; watch nudge_log flip from expo_error-dominant and tapped_at start appearing. Victor's pulse re-armed for 2026-07-19 ~07:30 EEST. Earlier: session 93b — City Riders Pulse DEPLOYED to production: migration applied, Cloud Run `defpedal-api-00115-dfv`, single-user test send verified on the consented test account; reach stays consent-gated on notify_riding_tips — 0 other registered users opted in at deploy time)

- **Session 95 (2026-07-19): Community-visibility ladder — Heartbeat + feeds widen honestly instead of rendering empty (4 commits, phases 1+2 → 3 → 4 → 5).** Root cause of "empty community": surfaces sliced by today+15 km at ~2.4 rides/day nationally (Bucharest probe: today/nearby=0 vs month/nearby=21), PLUS 176 badge + 13 tier `activity_feed` rows had `location=NULL` so `get_ranked_feed` showed them to followers only. **Hard rule kept: zero fabricated data — wider windows/radii only, honestly labeled.** (1) **Core** `communityVisibility.ts`: `CommunityWindow`/`CommunityScope`, named thresholds (`COMMUNITY_MIN_RIDES_PER_WINDOW=3`, `COMMUNITY_MIN_FEED_ITEMS=3`, nearby 15 km, region 100 km, feed-nearby 50 km — the ranked feed's historical radius is the no-regression floor, chart switch <7 rides/week, feed max-age 365d) + pure pickers with the documented 9-rung ladder (window widens before radius) — 17 tests. (2) **Migration `202607190001`** (LIVE): `get_community_pulse_counts` (9 window×scope ride counts, one scan), `get_activity_feed_scope_counts`; `get_city_heartbeat` rebuilt FROM THE LIVE DEF (repo migration had drifted — missing `is_hidden`/`is_anonymous` filters) with windowed/scoped `pulse`, `chartDaily`/`chartWeekly` (4×7d buckets), community-wide lifetime `communityTotals`, scope-aware `topContributors`; `get_ranked_feed` radius+max-age parameterized (defaults = old behavior, deployed-API-safe; old signatures DROPPED first — CREATE OR REPLACE with new params would create a PostgREST-ambiguous overload). (3) **API**: heartbeat resolves the rung server-side (counts RPC → core picker → data RPC; counts failure degrades to legacy today/nearby) returning `pulse`/`windowUsed`/`scopeUsed`/`chartMode`/`chartDaily`/`chartWeekly`/`communityTotals`; `/v2/feed` ladder 50→100→∞ km + 30d→365d recency with `scopeUsed` (+ per-page deterministic scope from counts, no cursor-format change); legacy `/feed` ladder 15→100→global with `scope` echo param for cursored pages; ALL new fields in the Fastify JSON Schemas (gotcha #9). (4) **Mobile**: Heartbeat pulse section labeled "Today/This week/This month in {city} / in your region / across the Defensive Pedal community" (9 explicit keys × EN+RO+ES — no string composition, RO reads naturally), PulseHeader honest title + rider label, ActivityChart weekly mode ("Last 4 weeks"), **lifetime community totals strip** as the first stat card (325 rides / 1,385 km / 166 kg CO2 / 81 riders — real rows, only ever go up), feed scope chip ("Showing rides from across the Defensive Pedal community"), `ActivityFeedCard` relative timestamps wired to the existing `feedCard.*` i18n keys (were hardcoded EN). All new heartbeat fields OPTIONAL in `CityHeartbeat` so persisted pre-ladder caches hydrate safely. (5) **Densify (`202607190002`, LIVE)**: `autoPublishBadgeUnlock`/`TierUp` stamp the user's latest located ride as `location` ONLY when `auto_share_rides=true` (sharing toggle gates stranger visibility; NULL stays follower-only; hazard hotspots deliberately NOT widened); backfill under the same consent rule → 167/176 badges + 11/13 tier-ups now located; `get_new_rider_count` RPC (real non-anonymous profiles, spatially attributed via their trip_shares, count-only) → `newRiders` on the first `/v2/feed` page → light `NewRidersCard` molecule (no map/reactions/user data) after the 2nd feed item; 18 real new riders community-wide this week. Fixed: v1.ts uses the exported session-94c `parseGeographyPoint`; `toPointWktOrNull` refuses 0/0 (NULL = follower-only, never a fabricated position); migration `202607190003` re-derived every 0,0 row from its parent trip / latest real ride (post-repair distribution clusters at Brașov/Bucharest/Cluj/Iași, zero at 0,0); #70 entry updated with the sweep rule (grep ALL consumers of a bitten column — `navigation_feedback.start_location` checked, it's a text column, clean). **Deploys: Cloud Run `defpedal-api-00120-7zw` (ladder) → `defpedal-api-00121-49h` (publish-path #70 fix, health OK); all three migrations live.** **E2E on production** (anonymous session, deployed API): Bucharest heartbeat → windowUsed=month/scopeUsed=nearby/chartMode=weekly, pulse 21 rides/17 riders, communityTotals 325/1,385 km/166 kg/81 riders; Bucharest feed 20 items (10 ride + 8 badge + 2 tier_up, scope nearby); London-vantage feed → full 20 items at scope 'community' + newRiders {count: 18}. - **Session 94b (2026-07-19): City Riders Pulse calibration — RO −60% + variable weather factor. Deployed Cloud Run `defpedal-api-00117-5zf` (health OK).** Trigger: Victor received his first live Bucharest pulse (~137k riders, mediocre Saturday) and judged it far too high. (1) **RO share** in `packages/core/src/cityPulse.ts` `COUNTRY_CYCLING_SHARE`: dedicated entry `{ share: 0.032, measured: false }` (was the shared 8% `ESTIMATED` default) → base rate 4.8%, jittered 4.08–5.52%; Bucharest same-conditions ~55k, summer envelope ~44k–116k. Side effect: RO towns <50k now sit BELOW the 9% small-town cap (cap no longer binds for RO; the cap-binding test example moved to PL Zakopane). (2) **Graded weather factor** (`getCityPulseWeatherFactor`): flat mediocre ×0.6 → continuous ×1.0→×0.4; per-dimension interpolation between the good-day limits (`CYCLING_*`) and the safety-suppression limits (`BAD_*` — NEW exports from `cyclingWeather.ts`, now also used inside `isBadCyclingWeather` so taper + safety floor share one source of truth); **worst dimension decides** (no averaging); floor ×0.4 at the suppression boundary; 2-decimal rounding for telemetry. 35% rain → ×0.9 (old cliff: ×0.6), 5°C dry → ×0.63, 3°C drizzle → ×0.47. `nudge_log.context.weatherFactor` now carries graded values — any dashboard filtering `= 0.6` must switch to ranges. Calibration history recorded in `docs/plans/city-riders-pulse-notification.md`. Tests: core 826 (new: RO rate bounds, taper mid-band/floor/worst-wins/monotonicity), mobile-api 601, typecheck 0. Deploy: Cloud Build `91dd6d10` → revision `defpedal-api-00117-5zf` 100% traffic.**
- **Session 94 (2026-07-18): Cycling-weather notification — randomized cadence (2x/day … once per 5 days) + day-3 inactivity escalation, replacing the fixed daily 8:30 ping. Shipped to Firebase `early-access-preview` as v0.2.117 (build 120), release `3brrscb7if8lo` — upload-key signer verified (82:7C:FD:44…), artefact audit passed; Victor confirmed receiving the notification on device (2026-07-19).** New pure module `apps/mobile/src/lib/daily-weather-schedule.ts` (29 tests): uniform 12h–120h interval draws build a **persisted chain** of fire times (`dailyWeatherChain` in Zustand, device-scoped, partialized) — persistence is load-bearing, an app open must NOT re-roll future draws or active users' delivered cadence collapses; every scheduling pass also pre-schedules **escalation fires at now+72/96/120/144h** (daily) which an app open/foreground cancels + recomputes, so they only reach users genuinely inactive ≥3 consecutive days (the requested "inactive 3 days → more frequent"); all fires snap forward into the 08:30–21:00 waking window, ≥6h apart, ≤12 scheduled. `daily-weather-notification.ts` rewritten: fetches an **8-day** Open-Meteo forecast (was 2), builds per-fire content via `forecastDayIndex` (same witty/safety `buildCyclingAdvice`), schedules the set under `daily-weather-cycling-<i>` ids, prefix-cancel via `getAllScheduledNotificationsAsync` also sweeps the legacy single `daily-weather-cycling` id on upgrade; fetch-fail still leaves the queued set intact; exports renamed to plural (`scheduleDailyWeatherNotifications` / `cancelDailyWeatherNotifications`). `DailyWeatherScheduler` now ALSO re-runs on AppState→active (15-min rate limit) so foregrounding counts as "used the app" for the escalation clock; only the mount pass may prompt for permission (foreground passes check silently — `ensureNotificationPermissionAsync` re-prompts while `canAskAgain`). Profile toggle-off now calls `cancelDailyWeatherNotifications()` (up to ~10 queued one-shots — stop-scheduling alone no longer suffices) and clears the chain. Dead helpers `computeTriggerSeconds`/`pickForecastIndex` removed from `daily-weather-messages.ts` (+ their tests). i18n copy de-daily-fied EN/RO/ES (`profile.dailyWeather*`). CLAUDE.md Notifications §4/§5 + Working Features updated. Mobile suite 1370 pass, typecheck 0, bundle 200, lint ratchet clean.
- **Session 93 (2026-07-17): City Riders Pulse nudge — IMPLEMENTED, NOT deployed (docs/plans/city-riders-pulse-notification.md, deployment steps appended to the plan).** New server-side trigger `city_riders_pulse` in the Pedal Nudge System: pushes “N people are cycling in {city} today” where N = population × rate × weekday × season × weather, deterministic per (city, date) via djb2 seeding (same helper as pedalVoice sticky buckets, now exported as `djb2Hash`). **Core** `cityPulse.ts`: `COUNTRY_CYCLING_SHARE` (31 countries, 8 measured Eurobarometer anchors ×3, rest 8% estimated ×1.5), rate clamp [0.5%, 40%] + 9% small-town cap (<50k), N floored at 40 + nearest-10-plus-seeded-offset rounding (RO “{n} de” grammar depends on the floor), weather factor good ×1.0 / mediocre ×0.6 / bad→suppressed (reuses isBadCyclingWeather/isGoodCyclingDay), `drawInitialFireAt`/`drawNextFireAt` (1–5 days, random minute in 07:00–21:30 local, fixed-offset math with the DST-correct quiet-hours gate as backstop), `isGuaranteeBreached` (5 days). **Dataset**: GeoNames cities15000 → `services/mobile-api/src/lib/nudges/citiesData.ts` (5,516 cities ≥15k in the 31 countries; generator `scripts/generate-cities-dataset.mjs`; deliberately NOT in core — Metro doesn’t tree-shake); `findNearestCity` 30km haversine scan, null → 100k-population fallback + pedalVoice’s localized “your city”. **Catalog**: 80 variants (EN/RO × sassy/neutral × 20) verbatim from the plan; per-send rotation djb2(userId+sendDate)%20 skipping the last 3 variant ids from nudge_log (voice stays sticky via pedal_voice_sassy; es renders EN until Spanish copy is commissioned). **Wiring**: `nudge_schedule` table (PK (user_id,trigger_id), RLS deny-all, migration `202607170001` — also widens the nudge_log trigger_id CHECK, live constraint name verified), Bucket D in the evaluate cron (due rows → candidate, P3; P2 via new `priorityOverrides` when guarantee breached), organic seeding (trips in last 7 days missing a row), schedule advance policy (sent → stamp+redraw; consent-off/anonymous/no-token/expo-error → redraw only; weather/sunset/quiet/cap/lost-slot → stay due, retry next tick), riding-tips consent gate for EVERYONE (registered too), full accounts only (NOT in ANONYMOUS_ALLOWED_TRIGGERS), safety floor via SAFETY_GATED_TRIGGERS, `CITY_PULSE_ENABLED` kill switch (default ON, `CITY_PULSE_ENABLED=false` in vitest env like NUDGES_ENABLED), attribution via ACTIONABLE_TRIGGERS. **Mobile**: one tap-handler case → route-planning (old builds already route via the generic nudge branch). **Tests**: +55 core (formula determinism/caps/floor/factors/window bounds/guarantee/rotation/no-raw-placeholder) and +19 mobile-api (nearest-city, eligibility gates, kill switch, P2 escalation); suites green: core 822, mobile-api 596, mobile 1356; typecheck 0; bundle 200. **NOT done (deliberate)**: no deploy, no migration applied, no Cloud Scheduler changes — manual steps + one-command rollback documented in the plan doc; honesty-valve estimate-wording flag out of scope. **UPDATE 2026-07-18 (session 93b): DEPLOYED + single-user tested.** Migration applied via MCP (live constraint swap verified), image built, revision `defpedal-api-00115-dfv` serving 100%. Test: victorrotariu@gmail.com consented (notify_riding_tips + consented_at stamped at his request), schedule row forced due, manual `nudges-evaluate-cron` run → nudge_log outcome `sent` 04:17:45Z, variant sassy-v6, context {n:136867, city:Bucharest, rate:0.1057, weatherFactor:0.6} — formula verified by hand (pop 1,877,155 × 10.57% × 1.15 Sat × 1.0 Jul × 0.6 ≈ 136,894 → 136,867 with seeded offset); schedule advanced (last_sent_at stamped, next draw +2d). - **Session 92 (2026-07-17): Navigation voice + HUD cleanup, collapsed preview sheet — v0.2.116 (build 119) to Firebase early-access-preview.** (1) **Off-route voice mute** — `speak()` in `app/navigation.tsx` now refuses to talk while `navigationSession.offRouteSince` is set. Root cause of the “voice keeps repeating the next instruction” complaint: while off-route `getNavigationProgress` recalculates the step index every GPS tick (`shouldRecalcStep`), which kept re-firing the pre/approach announcement flags. The one-time “off route” notice still plays (passes `allowWhenOffRoute: true`) and cuts mid-utterance speech via `Speech.stop()`; the pre/approach blocks additionally gate on `!progress.isOffRoute` so instructions aren’t marked-but-silent (they still fire once the rider rejoins the route); ManeuverCard tap repeats the instruction on demand even off-route; re-enabling the voice toggle while off-route arms voice without immediately reading the current step. Voice resumes automatically on rejoin or after a successful reroute (`offRouteSince` cleared). (2) **Route-preview summary sheet starts collapsed** — `CollapsibleSheet` in `MapStageScreen.tsx` now defaults to the peek strip (map-first); companion effect re-springs the collapsed height when `peekContent` appears after the async route load (sheet mounts before the route arrives — without it the peek row was clipped at handle-only height). Drag/tap/a11y behavior unchanged; route-preview is the sheet’s only consumer. (3) **Nav HUD menu removed** — the expanding menu FAB (History/Community/Profile) is gone from the ride HUD (mid-ride attention trap on handlebar mount; surfaces remain reachable post-ride); `showMenu` state + `nav.showMenu`/`nav.hideMenu` i18n keys dropped from en/ro/es. Typecheck 0; bundle 200; artefact audit passed; distributed to early-access-preview and verified on device.
- **Session 91 (2026-07-17): Analytics opt-in prompts (docs/plans/analytics-optin-prompts.md) — three contextual PostHog asks replace the removed onboarding toggle as the consent acquisition surface.** New `AnalyticsOptInCard` organism (Card base, ✕ 44pt, Mascot width 56 per-prompt pose, primary CTA + "No thanks" link + honest footer microline; opt-in sets `posthog: true` via `setAnalyticsConsent` — which stamps `capturedAt`, the Art 6(1)(a) consent record — records `convertedBy`, reverse fade/slide-out respecting reduced motion; parent shows the success Toast). **Pure gating** in `src/lib/analytics-optin.ts` (`shouldShowAnalyticsPrompt`): retired on PostHog-on or any recorded conversion, 2 dismissals anywhere = off forever, each prompt once ever, lifetime cap 3, 14-day spacing (fails closed on malformed timestamps). **Session arbitration** in one shared helper `src/lib/prompt-arbitration.ts` (`claimPromptSlot`): SaveRideCard > ReviewPromptCard > AnalyticsOptInCard; analytics never in the same session as either (bidirectional — if an analytics card showed first, save-ride/review yield for the session); SaveRide+Review coexistence unchanged; wired into all three call sites. **Store slice** `analyticsPrompt` `{asksShown, dismissCount, lastAskAt, convertedBy, impactDashboardVisits, hasReportedHazard}` — persisted, USER-scoped (reset in `resetUserScopedState`), Settings toggle-ON records `convertedBy:'settings'`. **Triggers:** (1) post-second-ride on the feedback impact step (exactly ride 2 — SaveRide's schedule is 1/3/8+5 so they can't collide on the same ride, but arbitration enforces it anyway); (2) post-first-hazard — **implementer's choice exercised per spec §prompt-2:** the route-planning "toast-adjacent slot" is contested territory (map-first screen, overlay system), so the prompt DEFERS to the next feedback-screen visit; evidence flag `markHazardReported()` set at all four hazard `enqueueMutation` sites (route-planning ×3, navigation ×1); (3) impact-dashboard 3rd+ visit (counter incremented on mount, eligibility latched once, card at the bottom of the scroll after Recent Badges/quiz card). i18n: full `analyticsOptIn` section EN/RO/ES with the spec's exact copy. 18 new unit tests (caps/spacing/retirement/trigger matrix/arbitration priority); mobile suite 1356 pass; typecheck 0; bundle 200; lint clean. **Shipped to Firebase as preview v0.2.114 (build 117), then v0.2.115 (build 118)** — v0.2.115 adds Diagnostics > "Growth prompts (dev)" (dual production gate like fake-GPS): full state readout (ride count, anonymous, analytics consent, save-ride shown/dismissals, analytics asks/lastAsk/convertedBy/dashboard-visits/hazard-flag) + a "Reset prompts + ride counter" button so the save-ride card and analytics prompts are retestable WITHOUT clearing app data. Built after the tester reported "no cards after two rides" — expected causes are all working-as-designed state (analytics toggled ON during the v0.2.111 test matrix retires all prompts; completedRideCount is a lifetime device counter so prompt 1's ride==2 rarely holds on a seasoned install; prior save-ride dismissals). Device verification pending on v0.2.115; if the readout shows an eligible state with no card, THAT is a bug.

- **Session 89 (2026-07-15): GPS-tracking audit (does tracking work for ALL trips?) + first fix shipped.** Full report `docs/reviews/gps-tracking-audit-2026-07-15.md` (rev 2) — 3 code-review agents + production SQL + Sentry release data. **Headline findings:** weekly track coverage collapsed ~100% (Apr) → 13% (Jul); dominant cause is **NavigationResumeGuard's Discard deleting the recorded trail** of interrupted rides (replaced the auto-save kill-recovery via the 2026-06-12 review; fielded ~Jun 17–27; `app_killed` recovery tracks 67 in May → 0 in July; 127 trackless "zombie" rides since Jun 15 — P1-0, fix = save-on-discard or 3-way prompt, NOT yet implemented). Code P0s: **anonymous-sign-in-failure rides never enqueued** (`route-preview.tsx:390` skips trip_start when `user==null`, `queueTripEnd` then bails — silent total loss, no retry of anon sign-in); **`resetUserScopedState` wipes unsynced trip mutations on ANY userId change** incl. the stale-refresh-token auto-recovery (`appStore.ts:1007` + `UserCacheResetBridge` — likely the residual ~33 stranded trips/month); **`/trips/track` missing the error-log #64 geometry defenses** — FIXED this session (see below). Also: 2000-crumb ring buffer truncates >~1h rides (production max trail is exactly 2000 pts); background-permission-denied riders lose locked-screen stretches silently (`useBackgroundNavigationSnapshot` wired but unread). Save path itself is healthy (0 saved-with-impact rides missing tracks since Jun 15; arrival-completed 98%). **Fleet correction (important for future sessions):** Sentry shows Play production runs **v0.2.92 (dominant since Jun 27, HAS the #60 fix) + v0.2.97 rolling since Jul 12** — "archived NOT uploaded" session notes ≠ fleet state; Victor uploads between sessions; check Sentry release health, not memory. **Shipped: `/trips/track` oversized-geometry hardening** (commit `06cb647`, Cloud Run **`defpedal-api-00111-q55`**, health+deep 200): 8 MiB route-scoped bodyLimit (shared `ROUTE_GEOMETRY_*` constants moved above the route), polyline cap 500k→6M chars, decode→downsample-to-15k→re-encode before storage (under-cap passes byte-identical; malformed drops the overlay never the trail); **app.ts error handler now preserves native Fastify 4xx statuses** (`FST_ERR_CTP_BODY_TOO_LARGE` was force-mapped to a retryable-looking 500 → offline queue burned 5 retries before dead-lettering). 4 new route tests; api suite 558 pass; live-probed on the revision (2 MiB body → parsed/400, 9 MiB → 413 + `BAD_REQUEST`/native code in details). Error-log **#65** (sweep payload-class fixes by input shape across ALL endpoints, not just the ones that alerted; error handlers must not convert permanent 4xx into retryable 500s; dead-letter-feeding endpoints deserve the most defensive limits). **Also shipped same session (mobile, rides the NEXT app build — commit `cf7c1a9`): P1-0 resume-prompt fix.** `NavigationResumeGuard` prompt is now three-way **Resume / Save ride / Discard ride** — "Save ride" runs the same close-out as automatic kill-recovery (trip_end + trip_track `app_killed`, background trail merged first) so an interrupted ride lands in History instead of being deleted; copy reframed "Resume navigation?" → "Finish your last ride?" and localized en/ro/es (old strings were hardcoded); footer stacked as a column (ro/es labels); `resume_guard_outcome` telemetry (auto_resume / auto_close_save / resume / save / discard) makes discard-vs-loss measurable. 9 component tests (new Save-ride case asserts trail survives with endReason app_killed); mobile 1223 pass; typecheck 0; bundle 200. **Both P0s shipped same session (mobile, ride the NEXT app build — commit `31aea0d`):** **P0-1** — trip_start now enqueues UNCONDITIONALLY in route-preview (the `if (user)` gate silently dropped whole rides when cold-start anonymous sign-in failed); `AuthSessionProvider` retries anonymous sign-in with backoff (10s→5min cap, re-checks the live session before each attempt so it never stacks a second anon user on an explicit sign-in; also covers mid-session stale-token sign-outs); `OfflineMutationSyncManager` gates the drain on a session existing (session-less requests would 401 → permanent 4xx → dead-letter) and re-flushes the moment one lands. **P0-2** — `resetUserScopedState` now PRESERVES queued `trip_start`/`trip_end`/`trip_track` on userId transitions (whole-chain rides upload under the next session; partially-synced chains 404 at resolve → dead-letter → RideLossBanner, visible not silent); user-scoped mutations (hazard votes, shares, feedback) still dropped; `tripServerIds` still cleared (a stale old-user id would make trip_end's owner-scoped UPDATE silently match 0 rows); persist force-flushed. 4 new tests; mobile 1227 pass. **Route-share 502 (user report, fixed + deployed — commit `629431f`, Cloud Run `defpedal-api-00112-gck`, error-log #66):** the session-84 SEC-6 CSPRNG hardening called `crypto.randomInt(0, 2 ** 48)` — Node's range cap is 2^48 − 1, so it threw `ERR_OUT_OF_RANGE` on EVERY call and `POST /v1/route-shares` 502'd 100% of the time since ~07-06 (15 Sentry events; hidden from tests because every test injects its own random source, and the real message only lives in Cloud Run `http_error_details` logs). Fixed with `randomBytes(6)` as exported `cryptoShareCodeRandomSource` + a regression test pinning the REAL production source. Reproduced 502 pre-deploy, verified 200 + valid code post-deploy (probe row cleaned), Sentry issue resolved with comment. **Audit backlog CLEARED same session (commit `88829e9`, mobile — rides the NEXT app build):** **P1-1** trail buffers thin (halve resolution, keep endpoints — core `thinBreadcrumbTrail`) instead of evicting oldest at cap, applied to BOTH the main 2000-crumb trail and the 1000-sample background locked-screen buffer — each pass doubles the holdable ride duration, no more losing the opening kilometres (`isPlausibleStep` stays valid, it self-calibrates to timestamp gaps); **P1-2** dismissible localized banner on the nav screen when screen-off recording is unavailable (background status was persisted but never read by UI; snapshot re-read 5s post-mount + 30s poll); **P0-3 client half** `boundRoutePolyline6` (`src/lib/routeGeometry.ts`, decode→12k downsample→re-encode, byte-identical under cap, never throws) at all three geometry upload sites (trip_track `plannedRoutePolyline6`, trip_share + route-share `geometryPolyline6`). New tests: core thinning ×4, routeGeometry ×3, appStore thinning behavior; all suites green; bundle 200. **Every finding from the 2026-07-15 GPS audit is now fixed** — server fixes live (`defpedal-api-00112-gck`), mobile fixes await the next build (fold into the v0.2.101+ release). **Same-day adversarial re-audit of these fixes** (`docs/reviews/session-89-fixes-re-audit-2026-07-15.md`, 3 reviewers) found **2 P1s in the new code, both fixed in `33e4da4`**: (1) ride-preservation misattribution — a departing REAL account's unsynced ride drained under the fresh anonymous user (silent + unrecoverable); now disposition-aware (`resetUserScopedState({rideDataDisposition})`: anon-previous → preserve, real-previous → dead-letter → RideLossBanner → post-sign-in retry attributes correctly); (2) Save-ride dedup hole — the already-queued-trip_end guard suppressed the trip_track enqueue on stale prompts (trail lost, telemetry lied); dedups now independent + `resetFlow` force-flushes persist (was the one flow-writer violating the June-22-cliff rule). - **Session 83 (2026-07-04): Daily Sentry sweep — 7 issues resolved, 2 ignored; DB migration + mobile fixes.** Connected Sentry MCP and triaged all unresolved issues. **DB fix (migration `202607040001_fix_retention_rpc_email_ambiguity.sql`, applied live):** Both retention RPCs had been failing every Monday since their April 28 deploy (first caught by Sentry on June 15). `flag_inactive_users` had `42702: column reference "email" is ambiguous` — PL/pgSQL `RETURNS TABLE(..., email text, ...)` creates an implicit output variable `email` that conflicts with bare `email` references inside the CTE; fixed by renaming the internal alias to `user_email` and adding `u.email::text` cast. `select_purgeable_inactive_users` had `42804: Returned type character varying(255) does not match expected type text in column 2` — `auth.users.email` is `varchar(255)` in Supabase but the function declares `email text`; fixed by casting `u.email::text`. Both verified post-migration by running the RPCs directly (clean empty arrays, no error). **Mobile fix MOBILE-4 (ExpoKeepAwake unhandled rejection, `commit bee666b`):** `deactivateKeepAwake` is typed `void` but the underlying native module resolves asynchronously — a synchronous `try/catch` misses rejections when the Android Activity is destroyed. Fixed with `void Promise.resolve(deactivateKeepAwake(KEEP_AWAKE_TAG)).catch(() => {})` to handle both sync and async rejection. **Mobile fix MOBILE-7 (trip_track sync timeout, `commit bee666b`):** `trip_track` inner timeout was 30s — too short for large GPS trails over cellular + Cloud Run cold starts (15–25s). Increased to 60s (outer safety net to 65s). Test table updated. **Mobile fix MOBILE-2 + MOBILE-C (Mapbox 422 distance limit, `commit 055e89a`):** Mapbox Directions API rejects cycling routes with straight-line distance >~400km with HTTP 422. Two surfaces fixed in `mapbox-routing.ts`: (1) the safe-mode comparison fast-route fetch now checks `haversineDistance([origin.lat, origin.lon], [destination.lat, destination.lon]) > 400_000` before calling Mapbox and skips silently; (2) the main fast/flat route path throws a clear user-facing error ("Route is too long for fast routing. Please switch to Safe routing.") instead of surfacing the 422. Note: `haversineDistance` takes `[lat, lon]` tuples, not `Coordinate` objects. **Resolved in Sentry:** MOBILE-K, MOBILE-M (retention RPCs), MOBILE-4, MOBILE-7, MOBILE-2, MOBILE-C. **Previously fixed / ignored:** MOBILE-H, MOBILE-N, MOBILE-J (already fixed/noise — marked in session 82). **No new API deploy** (all server fixes applied via Supabase migration; mobile fixes require a new build to reach users). Two commits pushed to `main`: `bee666b` (migration + navigation.tsx + offlineSyncHelpers) and `055e89a` (mapbox-routing.ts).
- **Session 82 (2026-07-04): Sentry audit + trip history 502 fix; Cloud Run defpedal-api-00101-f56.** Connected Sentry MCP and analysed all 13 unresolved issues. **P0 fixed:** `GET /v1/trips/history` was throwing 502 on every call (516 events, escalating, started June 29). Root cause: the calories feature added `ride_impacts(calories_burned)` as a PostgREST embedded resource join inside `getTripHistory`, but `ride_impacts.trip_id` references `trips`, not `trip_tracks` — there is no direct FK between `ride_impacts` and `trip_tracks`, so PostgREST rejected the join. Fix (`services/mobile-api/src/lib/submissions.ts`): two-query approach — fetch `trip_tracks` without the join, then fetch `ride_impacts WHERE trip_id IN (...)`, merge calories via Map. Calories still surface correctly. Deployed as Cloud Run **`defpedal-api-00101-f56`** (commit `5f70aa4`). Issue `DEFENSIVE-PEDAL-MOBILE-P` resolved in Sentry. **Already fixed, resolved in Sentry:** `MOBILE-H` (follow requests 502 — fixed session 75/76, last seen June 14), `MOBILE-N` (`.length` of undefined in `useApproachingRouteFeatures` — `?? []` guard already in code since v0.2.92), `MOBILE-J` (malformed JSON on merge-anonymous — `curl` test call, not a user). **Ongoing, monitoring:** `MOBILE-2` (39 users hitting Mapbox 422 "route exceeds max distance" — `handled:yes`, no crash; the fast-comparison `try-catch` catches it but Sentry tracing logs it; UX improvement: add straight-line distance guard before the comparison call to skip it for routes >400km — follow-up); `MOBILE-5` (21 events fatal crash `undefined is not a function`, build 94/v0.2.91, no source map — may be resolved in v0.2.92, monitor); `MOBILE-3` (Android view null, 2 users, intermittent native timing); `MOBILE-4` (ExpoKeepAwake.deactivate race, 1 event); `MOBILE-7` (trip_track sync timeout, 1 event); `MOBILE-G` (InstallReferrer Play SDK, 1 user, Android system service); `MOBILE-M/K` (retention cron 502s, 0 users — investigate separately).

- **Session 80 (2026-06-27): Trip-recording regression diagnosed + fixed → v0.2.92 shipped to API + preview + production-AAB + iOS TestFlight.** A silent `trip_tracks`-loss regression: GPS tracks not saved, rides stranded `in_progress`, missing from History/stats. Coverage fell from **~85% (pre-May-4) to 15% (week of Jun-22)** — **108 users / 190 trips** affected. **Root cause (3 stacked regressions):** the offline-queue trip flow (rolled out to the field ~May 4) made `trip_end`/`trip_track` resolve their server id **only** via the volatile, persisted `tripServerIds[clientTripId]` map; when that map was lost (app kill, `resetFlow` prune, or — Jun-13 — the new persist **debounce** with a fire-and-forget background flush), `getResolvedTripId` returned null → `isMutationReady` false → the mutation was **skipped on every flush forever**, never retried/killed/surfaced, stranding the trip `in_progress`. (Earlier May recovery via `useAppKilledRecovery` raced hydration; the Jun-13 debounce = the Jun-22 cliff.) Grounded in live-DB queries (per-week coverage, `null_client_id` correlating exactly with the rollout, `in_progress` vs terminal-no-track split). **Fix (commit `38b84ab`):** (1) **self-heal** — server `resolveTripIdByClientId` + `GET /v1/trips/resolve?clientTripId=` (requireWriteUser, read-only, owner-scoped, **un-rate-limited** so recovery can drain); client `OfflineMutationSyncManager` resolves a lost id from the durable `trips.client_trip_id` instead of dropping it (a 404 dead-letters → `RideLossBanner`); `isMutationReady`/`shouldSkipMutation` are now **queue-aware** (process an orphan when no `trip_start` is pending, still wait when one is). (2) **durable persist** — `flushPersistedWrites()` after trip-critical queue/map mutations in `queueSlice.ts` (`enqueueMutation`/`resolveMutation`/`killMutation`/`setTripServerId`/`setActiveTripClientId`) so the queue + id-map survive a hard kill despite the 3s/8s debounce; GPS-breadcrumb churn stays debounced. **On first launch of a build with the fix, orphaned mutations still in a device's queue self-heal and retroactively create the missing `trip_tracks`.** **Old 310 unrecorded trips left as-is** (decided NOT to backfill — `trips` has no geometry column, the actual GPS trail was never sent server-side; only on-device queue copies are recoverable, via the shipped fix). **Tests:** `offlineSyncHelpers` (queue-aware readiness + `hasPendingTripStart`), `submissions` (`resolveTripIdByClientId`), completed 4 `lib/storage` mocks. **Verified:** typecheck (3 workspaces), mobile-api **523**, mobile suites, `check:bundle` 200, lint ratchet 0. **Shipped:** API live on Cloud Run **`defpedal-api-00099-qns`** (`/v1/trips/resolve`, `/health/deep` 200); **preview 0.2.92 (95)** → Firebase `early-access-preview`; **production AAB 0.2.92 (95)** built + verified-signed with the upload key (`keytool -printcert` SHA-256 `82:7C:FD:…:35:73`, `jarsigner` "jar verified"), archived `apkreleases/DefensivePedal-Production-v0.2.92.aab`, **NOT uploaded** (confirm vc 95 > live prod vc first; staged rollout); **iOS build 17 (v0.2.92)** built on EAS + submitted → **`VALID` on TestFlight** (ASC 6778694757, buildNumber 16→17, clean non-interactive run, no new blockers), **not yet promoted to App Store review**. Commits `38b84ab` (fix) + `b0a219b` (release/0.2.92 bump + release notes + CLAUDE.md "always archive the AAB to `apkreleases/`" rule) pushed to `main`; pre-push hook green; **git now matches prod API + builds**.
- **Session 79 (2026-06-25): Two more App Store review rejections fixed — 5.1.1(iv) (location skip button) + 2.1(a) (Google sign-in error on iOS).** Both fixed graceful-handling-only (no native/API/schema changes); verified `npm run typecheck` (3 workspaces) + `npm run lint:mobile:check` (no regressions) + `npm run check:bundle` HTTP 200; staged for the next iOS build (EAS auto-increments from build 15). Runbook log + App Review reply text for each in `docs/runbooks/ios-app-store-submission.md`.
  - **5.1.1(iv) — pre-permission skip/exit removed.** After build 15 went VALID and was reviewed, Apple re-rejected the SAME onboarding location screen (`apps/mobile/app/onboarding/index.tsx`) — this time the *skip affordances*, not the button verb (*"the user can close the message and delay the permission request with the 'Skip for now' or 'Skip' button… the user should always proceed to the permission request after the message"*). The screen had two bypasses: the top-right `skipPill` (`useSkipOnboarding`) and a footer "Skip" link (`handleSkip`, which routed to consent without ever calling `requestForegroundPermissionsAsync()`). **Fix (both platforms, single code path):** removed both — the screen now has exactly one forward action, the "Continue" button, which always invokes the OS prompt. The denied branch is unchanged (compliant — it appears *after* the request) and gained an **"Open Settings"** link (`Linking.openSettings()`, Apple-permitted recovery). Onboarding-skip survives overall — `onboarding/consent.tsx` (the next screen) keeps its own skip pill, so users can still exit one step later, after passing through the prompt. New i18n `onboarding.openSettings` (EN/RO/ES). Regression guard `apps/mobile/src/__tests__/app/onboarding-permission.test.tsx` (3 tests). `vitest.mock-rn.ts` `Linking` gained `openSettings`.
  - **2.1(a) — Google sign-in clock-skew error on iOS.** On iPhone 17 Pro Max / iOS 26.5, Google sign-in showed a raw red `RNGoogleSignIn … Error Domain=org.openid.appauth.general Code=-15 "Issued at time is more than 600 seconds before or after the current time"`. **Root cause:** the GoogleSignIn iOS SDK (AppAuth/OpenID) validates the Google ID token's `iat` against the DEVICE clock with a hardcoded ±600s tolerance; the review device's clock was >10 min off, so the token was rejected on-device before reaching Supabase, and `auth.tsx` rendered the raw `error.message`. No JS-level leeway config in google-signin v16; **Android unaffected** (Credential Manager token carries no client `iat` check) → iOS-only device-clock issue. **Fix (graceful + proactive, no browser fallback):** `lib/supabase.ts` `classifyGoogleSignInError()` → stable `errorCode` (`clock_skew`/`unavailable`/`no_token`/`configuration`/`generic`); `signInWithGoogle()` returns the code and never surfaces the raw string; added `GoogleSignin.signOut()` before the interactive `signIn()` so retries mint a fresh token. New `lib/clockSkew.ts` `getServerClockSkewSeconds()` compares the device clock to the mobile API's HTTP `Date` header (non-blocking, null on failure). `auth.tsx` maps `errorCode` → localized message (no raw dumps) + a proactive warning banner when skew ≥ 300s. i18n EN/RO/ES `googleClockSkew`/`googleUnavailable`/`googleGenericError`/`clockSkewBanner` (`{{minutes}}`). Tests `src/lib/__tests__/{googleSignInError(6),clockSkew(9)}.test.ts`. **Caveat:** if the reviewer's device clock is still off on retest, native Google still won't *succeed* (only a server-validated web-OAuth fallback would force that — deliberately not added per error-log #26/#27); but the broken-error UX is gone, pre-warned, and Apple/email sign-in work. Reviewer reply makes the clock-skew root cause explicit.
  - **Build 16 shipped to App Store Connect + CI made green again.** Committed `eb189ea`, pushed; built iOS production **build 16** (v0.2.91, build ID `99b670d2-…`) via EAS from Windows, submitted to ASC (submission `a7a6d28b-…`), verified `processingState=VALID` via the ASC builds API (ES256 JWT). The push's CI run failed on the **Security audit** step (NOT typecheck/lint — the pre-push hook doesn't run `audit:ci`, per error-prevention #17): a newly-published HIGH advisory **`GHSA-vxpw-j846-p89q`** (undici WebSocket-client DoS) reaching production deps via `@sentry/react-native → @sentry/cli → undici@6.24.1`. `@sentry/cli` is build-time source-map tooling (never in the shipped Hermes app) and the WebSocket path is unreachable; `npm audit fix` is destructive here (its dry-run removes vitest/jsdom/@types/react). **Allowlisted** in `scripts/audit-ci.mjs` with a documented reason (+ updated the error-prevention #17 example list); `npm run audit:ci` green.
- **Session 78 (2026-06-17): App Store rejection 5.1.1(iv) — location-permission button wording.** Apple rejected the first App Store submission (**v1.0 build 14**, reviewed 2026-06-17, submission `10455ac9-…`) under **Guideline 5.1.1(iv)**: the onboarding pre-permission screen (`apps/mobile/app/onboarding/index.tsx`) explains why location is used, then has a primary button that triggers the OS dialog — but the button said **"Enable Location"**, a directive verb Apple treats as "encouraging/directing" the user to grant access. Apple's exact fix: use a neutral word like **"Continue"** or **"Next"**. **Fix = string-only, all 3 locales** (`enableLocation` key): EN `Enable Location → Continue`, ES `Activar ubicación → Continuar`, RO `Activează locația → Continuă`. Component logic untouched — the button still calls `requestForegroundPermissionsAsync()`, the explanatory copy stays (Apple permits explaining *why* before the prompt), and the denied-state / Skip paths are unchanged. The other location call sites (`useCurrentLocation`, `useForegroundNavigationLocation`) are runtime requests fired on actual feature use, not directive pre-prompts, so they're outside this guideline. **Version note:** repo `version` has always been `0.2.91` (never `1.0`); EAS `appVersionSource:"remote"` manages only the build number (→ 15). The reviewer's "1.0" is the App Store Connect version *record*; build 14 (same 0.2.91 repo) attached to it, so build 15 attaches identically — no version edit needed. **Verified:** `npm run typecheck` clean (3 workspaces), `npm run check:bundle` HTTP 200, no test references the old string. Rebuilt as iOS production build 15 for resubmission to the existing 1.0 record + reviewer reply noting the wording change.
- **Session 78 cont. (2026-06-18): post-rejection work — App Store resubmit, a production crash OTA, and a CI security-gate fix.** After the 5.1.1(iv) fix shipped, three follow-ons: **(1) iOS build 15 resubmitted** — built (auto-incr 14→15), `eas submit` (first attempt stuck `IN_QUEUE` ~53 min with no error → cancelled via GraphQL `cancelSubmission` → resubmitted `f2bdffbf`), Apple processing → **build 15 VALID** at ASC; user resubmitted for review. Headless verification via the ASC API (ES256 JWT) + EAS GraphQL is captured in `docs/runbooks/ios-app-store-submission.md`. **(2) Sentry `d99b1306` crash fixed (`c766b33`)** — `useApproachingRouteFeatures` did `selectedRoute.routeFeatures.length` unguarded; a `routePreview` persisted by a pre-v0.2.55 build hydrates without `routeFeatures` (undefined at runtime despite the required type) → `Cannot read property 'length' of undefined` mid-navigation. Fix = `?? []` guard mirroring `useFeatureCollections.ts:109`, + regression test. Shipped to Android prod via the **first-ever production EAS Update OTA** (group `e3f7e63b`, rv `0.2.25`, android-only). **OTA gotchas (memory `reference_eas-update-ota.md`):** runtimeVersion is frozen at `0.2.25` in the hand-managed Android `strings.xml` (no `expo prebuild`), so OTA needs a temp rv pin to reach the fleet, and `--rollout-percentage` can't stage on a fresh branch (went 100%, not 10%). Rollback armed (`eas update:roll-back-to-embedded`). **(3) CI Security-audit fix (`scripts/audit-ci.mjs`)** — `npm audit --omit=dev --audit-level=high` began failing on two newly-published HIGH advisories in transitive dev/telemetry tooling (`ws` via Expo/Metro dev-server `GHSA-96hv-2xvq-fx4p`; `protobufjs` via posthog→@opentelemetry `GHSA-wcpc-wj8m-hjx6`) — unrelated to any code, would break any push. npm `overrides` silently won't rewrite those nested workspace sub-trees in npm 11, and `npm audit fix` rips out `@opentelemetry/core` (breaks `@sentry/node`, 12 mobile-api suites). Replaced the bare audit with `npm run audit:ci` → a dependency-free gate that fails on any high/critical EXCEPT a small inline-documented allowlist of those two non-shipped advisories. Verified exit 0 with allowlist, exit 1 without; full local suite (contrast 32, validate, ~1885 unit tests across core+mobile) green before push.
- **Session 77 (2026-06-14): iOS + Android polish — impact-card clip, TestFlight build 13, Google sign-in, review prompt, Safe default.** Five fixes, all pushed to `main`. **(1) Impact-card number clipping on iOS (`fix(mobile): 1b8aa46`).** The big ride-impact numbers (`0.0 ML` / `0.00 kg` / `EUR 0.00`) in `ImpactSummaryCard.tsx`'s `StaggeredCounter` rendered through `AnimatedCounter`, which merges the `textDataMd` token (`fontSize 20`, `lineHeight 24`) with the caller style — but the caller overrode `fontSize` to **28** without raising `lineHeight`. A 28px glyph inside a 24px line box → iOS clips the digit tops & bottoms (Android is forgiving, so it only showed on the Apple build). Fix = pass `lineHeight: 34` (~1.2×) alongside the `fontSize: 28` override. Swept all other large-font sites — this was the only one spreading a tight-lineHeight token under a bigger fontSize; the rest set their own lineHeight or spread no token (RN computes a safe default). **(2) EAS iOS `pod install` failure (`fix(ios): e7abe91`).** Build 12 (the first attempt with fix #1) **errored at the Install pods phase**: `@react-native-google-signin/google-signin ^16` now resolves a GoogleSignIn pod that transitively pulls the **Swift pod `AppCheckCore`**, which can't link as a static library unless `GoogleUtilities` + `RecaptchaInterop` define Clang modules. No `Podfile.lock` is committed (no `ios/`; EAS prebuilds fresh each build), so this regressed via **transitive pod version drift** since the green build 11 (2026-06-11) — nothing in our code changed it. Fix = new iOS config plugin `apps/mobile/plugins/withIosGoogleModularHeaders.js` (`withDangerousMod`) that injects `:modular_headers => true` for GoogleUtilities / RecaptchaInterop / AppCheckCore into the generated Podfile after `use_expo_modules!`. Chose the targeted modular-headers remedy (the one CocoaPods itself suggests) over the heavier `useFrameworks: "static"` hammer, which would change linkage for every pod and risk NEW failures deep in the Xcode build — this keeps the rest of the build byte-identical to build 11. **Build trail:** build 12 (commit `1b8aa46`) ❌ pod install → build 13 (commit `e7abe91`, v0.2.91, auto-incremented build number) ✅ FINISHED on EAS → `eas submit` ✅ uploaded to App Store Connect. ASC processing verified VALID via the App Store Connect API (ES256 JWT) — a successful upload can still be Apple-rejected during processing (cf. build 10 ITMS-90771), so trust the API, not the upload. **(3) iOS Google Sign-In nonce mismatch (Supabase config — no code change).** iOS Google sign-in failed with *"Passed nonce and nonce in id_token should either both exist or not."* Root cause (verified against GoTrue source): on iOS the GoogleSignIn SDK bakes a nonce into the id_token returned by `@react-native-google-signin/google-signin` v16.1.2's classic `GoogleSignin.signIn()`, but the app calls `signInWithIdToken({ provider:'google', token })` with no nonce → GoTrue's `tokenHasNonce != paramsHasNonce` XOR check trips. **No viable code fix:** v16.1.2 is the latest and exposes **no nonce API / no `GoogleOneTapSignIn`**, so the digest can't be controlled; the "decode the token's nonce and pass it back" trick can't work either (GoTrue SHA-256-hashes whatever you pass before comparing). Fix = enable **"Skip nonce checks"** on the Supabase Google provider (Authentication → Providers → Google). Server-side only, no rebuild — existing build 13 works once flipped. Low security cost on a native flow (token still validated for signature/aud/iss/exp; never traverses a browser). **HARD RULE:** never add a nonce to the Google `signInWithIdToken` call — with Skip-nonce ON it re-creates the mismatch. Apple sign-in is unaffected (it uses a real controlled nonce). Captured in memory `reference_ios-google-signin-nonce.md`. **(4) Android review prompt opens Play Store (`fix(mobile): 90b47f8`).** The "rate" CTA called Google's in-app `ReviewManager` (`expo-store-review`), which only renders on Play-installed builds, is quota-limited, and **resolves successfully even when it shows nothing** — so `requestReview()` returned `'native'` and the Play Store fallback never fired; most users saw nothing. Android now opens the Play Store listing directly (`market://` → `https` fallback) so the user always reaches a review surface. iOS keeps the native SKStoreReview sheet + write-review URL fallback. JS-only. **(5) Safe is now the real default routing profile (`fix(mobile): ef82458`).** The store default AND an existing `v1→v2` persist migration both already set `mode:'safe'`, but a `route-planning.tsx` `useEffect` force-set `'fast'` whenever `resolvedCountry.routeSupported` was false — which is ALSO false on the empty planning screen (no destination yet) and during GPS resolution, so it overwrote `'safe'`→`'fast'` on nearly every cold start, silently undoing the migration. Fix = gate the force-fast on a **destination actually being set** (no destination = no route to downgrade, so the Safe default stands; cross-border / out-of-coverage routes still flip to Fast once a destination is picked) + a `v3→v4` persist migration that re-applies `mode:'safe'` to heal the bug-residue `'fast'` already persisted on existing installs (`'flat'` riders untouched). **Verified:** `npm run typecheck` clean (3 workspaces), `npm run check:bundle` HTTP 200, all 92 `appStore` tests pass, lint ratchet 0. **Note:** the impact-card fix is iOS-render-specific — Android can't show the regression, so on-device TestFlight is the confirmation surface. The Supabase Skip-nonce toggle is a dashboard action (done by Victor), not in the repo.
- **Session 76 (2026-06-13/14): Review backlog — Section B (2 of 3 tractable items; 3 commits pushed; Sentry deployed live).** Continued `docs/reviews/full-app-review-2026-06-12-HANDOFF.md` "What's LEFT → B. High-value, tractable, no device needed". **(1) Dead-letter ride-loss recovery banner (`feat: 9dc0c3b`, mobile-only).** A dead `trip_start` cascade-kills the whole ride's server record (`OfflineMutationSyncManager`), and the only prior recovery path was the dev Diagnostics screen — riders had no way to retry a lost ride. New `RideLossBannerManager` in `app/_layout.tsx` shows an elevated danger banner when there's an undismissed dead trip-critical mutation (`trip_start/trip_end/trip_track/feedback`); **suppressed during NAVIGATING** (never overlay the live HUD). Retry → `retryDeadMutations()` (re-queues all dead → the 15s sync loop re-attempts); Dismiss → session-local hide tracked by mutation id (re-appears next launch if still unsynced — non-destructive, appropriate for a data-loss warning; a *new* dead ride re-triggers after a prior dismiss). New `RideLossBanner` molecule + pure `lib/rideLoss.ts` selectors (`selectDeadCriticalMutations`/`hasUndismissedRideLoss`, 6 tests) + `rideLoss.*` i18n keys en/ro/es (parity type-enforced). **(2) Sentry error tracking on the Fastify API (`feat(api): 790c2e5`, server-only).** API 500s were only visible in Cloud Run logs — no alerting/grouping/release-health. Added `@sentry/node@^10.57.0`; new `lib/sentry.ts` (`initSentry` gated on `SENTRY_DSN`, `captureServerException` no-op wrapper, `flushSentry`), `instrument.ts` imported first in `server.ts` (canonical setup — init before Fastify/http load), `captureServerException` for **5xx only** in `app.ts` setErrorHandler (covers cron fatals — they throw HttpError 500 to the central handler), the two non-throwing 5xx sites in `v1.ts` (push-token register, admin notification send) instrumented directly, and Sentry's default Node integrations auto-capture uncaught exceptions + unhandled rejections (the fire-and-forget nudge/push paths). `config.sentry { dsn, environment, release=K_REVISION, tracesSampleRate=0 }`; `.env.example` documented. **ACTIVATED 2026-06-14:** built + deployed to Cloud Run revision **`defpedal-api-00094-qg7`** (100% traffic, `/health` + `/health/deep` both 200) with `SENTRY_DSN` set via `--update-env-vars` (all 17 env vars preserved). DSN **reuses the mobile Sentry project** (`o4511290594754561.ingest.de.sentry.io/4511290618544208`, EU) per Victor's call — server events separable by `environment=production` (auto from baked NODE_ENV) + `release=<revision>` (auto from K_REVISION) + the node SDK tag. A dedicated API Sentry project is the clean-up-later option. Rollback: redeploy a prior revision or unset `SENTRY_DSN` (init self-skips → no-op). **(3) Trip-history payload diet — DEFERRED (was listed under B but isn't device-free).** Investigation: `GET /v1/trips/history` ships `gps_trail` (≤50 trips × ≤2000 pts), but `TripCard` renders the trail map **on expand** in the list and uses the trail as a **distance fallback** when `actual_distance_meters` is null, plus 5 more consumers (share card, GPX export, trip-map, trip-compare, trip/[id]). Dropping it needs a new per-trip trail endpoint + rewiring all of them, and the expand-to-replay path effectively requires device verification — not the "no device needed" the handoff assumed. Left for a device-equipped session. **Verified:** full `npm run typecheck` clean (3 workspaces), mobile `rideLoss` 6/6, full API suite **515/515** (512 baseline + 3 new Sentry tests), `npm run check:bundle` HTTP 200, lint ratchet 0, `npm audit --omit=dev --audit-level=high` exit 0 (@sentry/node added only moderate prod advisories). **Manual-test debt:** the ride-loss banner's appearance/Retry/Dismiss is device-only (force a dead trip mutation); banner reaches devices on next preview/prod build. **Deployed:** Sentry only (Cloud Run `defpedal-api-00094-qg7`).
- **Session 76 cont. (2026-06-14): API Sentry validated in prod + first bug it caught, fixed & deployed.** Within minutes of the Sentry deploy, a real production 500 alerted by email — **`GET /v1/profile/follow-requests`** firing repeatedly. **Root cause:** the handler embedded `profiles!user_follows_follower_id_fkey(...)`, but that FK references `auth.users(id)`, not `public.profiles` → PostgREST "Could not find a relationship between 'user_follows' and 'profiles'". **Broken since it shipped** — every account with a pending follow request 500'd; previously invisible (logs only), now caught instantly. This is exactly Sentry's value. **Fix (`fix(api): 0b2d33d`, deployed `defpedal-api-00095-t9t`):** dropped the impossible embed, fetch pending `user_follows` rows then batch-fetch `profiles` by follower id + in-memory join — the same workaround `activity-feed.ts` already documents for this identical FK-points-to-auth.users trap (verified follow.ts was the ONLY remaining offender via `profiles!` grep). Response shape unchanged; success test updated to the two-query mock; full API 515/515. `/health` + `/health/deep` 200, SENTRY_DSN preserved. **Forgot-password email (the item Victor was actually testing) — NOT a code bug:** Supabase Auth logs show `POST /recover` → **200** (561ms) for victorrotariu@gmail.com from the preview app (`scheme=defensivepedal-preview`); no mailer/SMTP/rate-limit error logged. Supabase accepted the request and handed it to its mailer → **non-delivery is a Supabase email-delivery issue** (built-in email service deliverability/hourly rate-limit, or spam), fixable only from the Supabase dashboard (configure custom SMTP / check rate limits / check spam). **Dev tooling:** added a "Force dead trip mutation (banner test)" button to the Diagnostics "Developer validation" card (dev/preview only) so the ride-loss banner can be triggered on demand (`test(dev)` commit).

- **Session 75e (2026-06-13): Review Phase 4 — perf & polish (highest-value subset; 2 commits).** **Perf:** (1) debounced the Zustand persist adapter (`lib/storage.ts`) — during nav the store was written on every GPS sample (~1/2s, twice) with the 2000-crumb ring buffer + full route geometries in the persisted slice, so a ride churned dozens of full partialize+JSON.stringify+AsyncStorage writes/min on the JS thread; now a trailing debounce (3s, 8s max-wait) coalesces them, `flushPersistedWrites()` fires on app-background so an OS kill loses nothing, and the Phase 3 background trail backstops breadcrumbs. Factored as testable `createDebouncedStorage`; disabled under vitest (the global async-storage mock made it active in all store tests, leaving dangling timers → flaky cross-file failures). (2) Trophy Case FlatList virtualization (initialNumToRender/maxToRenderPerBatch/windowSize/removeClippedSubviews) — 140+ HoloSticker cells were all mounted up front. **a11y:** Button fixed-`height`→`minHeight`+padding (label clipping at large OS font scale); MapStageScreen sheet handle (PanResponder-driven, screen-reader-invisible) got button role + label + expanded state. **i18n:** foreground-service lock-screen notification (most-visible string during screen-off rides) localized via the locale store at ride start. **Observability:** new `GET /health/deep` readiness probe — cheap Supabase round-trip (head count on profiles) returning 503 on failure, so an uptime monitor can tell "process up" from "up but every request fails"; `/health` stays shallow for Cloud Run liveness. (3) `killServiceOnDestroy: true` on the foreground service — it defaulted false + START_REDELIVER_INTENT, so swipe-away mid-ride leaked the service (persistent notification + GPS drain) until reboot; now swipe-away stops it while a memory-kill still resumes. Clears the trail on ride start so prior rides can't leak into the merge. **Offline map packs:** (1) real `createdAt` baked into pack metadata — `toStatus` stamped `updatedAt` as the moment of LISTING so every pack looked ~0ms old: the 5-day auto-delete NEVER fired and LRU compared identical timestamps; now age + LRU work (legacy packs fall back to fresh). - Session 73 (2026-06-09): **Two production fixes — CI green + install-referrer crash.** Triggered by a Sentry crash email + failing GitHub CI. **(1) CI:** the Security audit step (`npm audit --audit-level=high`) had failed on every push since ~June 3 — a **dev-only** critical advisory (vitest ≤3.2.5, GHSA-5xrq-8626-4rwp, Vitest UI server arbitrary file read/exec; fix is vitest 4 major). It never ships. Changed `.github/workflows/ci.yml` to `npm audit --omit=dev --audit-level=high` so CI audits only production (shipped) deps; verified exit 0 (15 moderate dev-tool advisories remain, none ship). error-prevention #17 updated. **(2) Crash (`IllegalStateException: Service not connected` at `PlayInstallReferrer.java:49` → `Thread.run`):** `react-native-play-install-referrer` reads the install referrer on its OWN background thread; `getInstallReferrer()` throws `IllegalStateException` when the Play service disconnects mid-read, and the library's `try` only catches `RemoteException` → uncaught background-thread throw → crash. `src/lib/installReferrer.ts`'s JS guards can't catch a native-thread throw. **Fixed via patch-package** (new infra: `patch-package` devDep + root `postinstall`): `patches/react-native-play-install-referrer+1.1.9.patch` widens `catch (RemoteException ex)` → `catch (Exception ex)`, so it reports a JS error event instead of crashing. **Build integration:** the release build copies to `C:\dpb` and skips `npm install` when current, so `scripts/build-preview.sh` now robocopies `patches/` to DST and runs `npx patch-package` explicitly (Step 1a2) with a grep assertion that the patch landed. patch-package gotcha logged (the lib's npm tarball ships stray `android/build/` artifacts → trim the patch to the source hunk only). error-log #56. **Verification:** patch round-trips (reverse→`RemoteException`, apply→`Exception`); typecheck clean; bundle HTTP 200; `npm audit --omit=dev --audit-level=high` exit 0. **NOTE:** the crash fix is a NATIVE change — the already-built **v0.2.90 AAB predates it**; a production rebuild folds it in (recommended before uploading v0.2.90, since it's not yet on Play). **(3) Unmasked test failures:** fixing the audit step let CI reach "Run unit tests" for the first time in ~2 weeks, exposing 7 pre-existing failing mobile test files (the documented "weather.test + badge/share render crashes" from session 69 — broken RN test harness: StyleSheet.create undefined, Flow `import typeof` collection errors, getWeatherWarnings undefined under the harness). Not code regressions (production paths run fine at runtime/on-device); confirmed not caused by this session's changes. Quarantined them in `apps/mobile/vitest.config.ts` exclude (extending the existing 3-file pattern) so CI is a real gate again for the other ~2260 tests. After exclusion: mobile 1018 ✓ / core 733 ✓ / mobile-api 516 ✓, 0 failures. **TODO (tracked):** repair the RN test harness / mock shim and re-enable the 7 files. **UPDATE (same day): RN harness restored — ALL 7 re-enabled (mobile suite 1018 → 1100).** Root causes were missing mocks: added `Image` + `PanResponder` to `vitest.mock-rn.ts` (HoloSticker's `PanResponder.create` was the "undefined.create" crash), and comprehensive `react-native-svg` + `expo-clipboard` mocks to `vitest.setup.ts` (the Flow `import typeof` collection errors). Also removed redundant/incomplete local `vi.mock('react-native-svg')` from 3 test files (now use the canonical setup mock) and made `useShareRoute.test.ts`'s `react-native` mock spread the shim (it had dropped `Platform`). Re-enabled: useShareCard, useShareRoute, BadgeCard, ImpactSummaryCard, BadgeInlineChip (+32 tests; mobile suite 1018→1050).
